# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="17fb2-102">Types obsolètes dans le .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="17fb2-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>

<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="17fb2-103">Les tableaux de cet article listent les types obsolètes dans .NET Framework 4.5 et .NET Framework 4.6, organisés par assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="17fb2-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and the .NET Framework 4.6, organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="17fb2-104">Utilisez les liens suivants pour consulter la liste des types obsolètes et des alternatives recommandées dans chaque assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="17fb2-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="17fb2-105">Ces types étant obsolètes, tous leurs membres le sont également.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="17fb2-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="17fb2-106">Pour obtenir la liste des membres obsolètes supplémentaires dans la bibliothèque de classes .NET Framework, consultez [Membres obsolètes](obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="17fb2-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

## <a name="obsolete-types-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="17fb2-133">Types obsolètes dans les assemblys système</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="17fb2-133">Obsolete Types in System Assemblies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="17fb2-134">Les tableaux suivants répertorient les types qui ont été déclarés obsolètes dans les assemblys système.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="17fb2-134">The following tables list the types that have been declared obsolete in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="17fb2-135">Ces assemblys sont utilisés pour le développement d’applications à usage général qui ciblent le .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="17fb2-135">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>
